OBJECT Report 51103 Import Loc. 4 (DD) Files
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=07/01/20;
    Time=12:00:00 AM;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Import Loc. 4 (DD) Files;
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   LocationCode := '4';
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  WhseReleaseLine.LOCKTABLE;
                  WhseReleaseLine.DELETEALL;
                END;

    OnPostReport=BEGIN
                   WhseReleaseLine.DELETEALL;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1000000000;;DataItem;xFile             ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000022;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Path,Is a file,Name)
                                 WHERE(Path=CONST(U:\WAREHOUSE FILES\CKDORMAN\),
                                       Is a file=CONST(Yes));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CommonInpFile.TEXTMODE(FALSE);
                                  CommonInpFile.OPEN(xFile.Path + xFile.Name);

                                  STOn := FALSE;
                                  i := 0;
                                  j := 0;
                                  k := 0;
                                  l := 1;
                                  CLEAR(CKElement[l]);
                                  CLEAR(CodeString);

                                  REPEAT
                                    IF CommonInpFile.READ(Char) = 0 THEN
                                      j := 1;

                                    i := i + 1;

                                    IF Char = 42 THEN BEGIN
                                      k := 0;
                                      CKElement[l] := CodeString;
                                      CLEAR(CodeString);
                                      l := l + 1;
                                      CLEAR(CKElement[l]);
                                    END ELSE
                                      IF Char = 126 THEN BEGIN
                                        k := 0;
                                        CKElement[l] := CodeString;
                                        CLEAR(CodeString);
                                        l := l + 1;

                                        CASE CKElement[1] OF
                                          'GS':
                                            BEGIN
                                              EVALUATE(
                                                BatchDate,
                                                COPYSTR(CKElement[5],3,2) + '/' +
                                                COPYSTR(CKElement[5],5,2) + '/' +
                                                COPYSTR(CKElement[5],1,2));
                                              EVALUATE(BatchTime,CKElement[6]);
                                            END;
                                          'BEG':
                                            BEGIN
                                              EVALUATE(ExternalDocumentNo,CKElement[4]);
                                              EVALUATE(ReleaseNo,CKElement[5]);
                                              EVALUATE(
                                                OrderDate,
                                                COPYSTR(CKElement[6],5,2) + '/' +
                                                COPYSTR(CKElement[6],7,2) + '/' +
                                                COPYSTR(CKElement[6],1,4));

                                              FreightChargeAmt := 0;
                                            END;
                                          'DTM':
                                            EVALUATE(
                                              ShipmentDate,
                                              COPYSTR(CKElement[3],5,2) + '/' +
                                              COPYSTR(CKElement[3],7,2) + '/' +
                                              COPYSTR(CKElement[3],1,4));
                                          'SAC':
                                            IF (CKElement[3] = 'D240') THEN BEGIN
                                              EVALUATE(FreightChargeAmt,CKElement[6]);
                                              FreightChargeAmt := ROUND(FreightChargeAmt / 100,0.01);
                                            END;
                                          'TD5':
                                            ShippingAgentAndService := CKElement[6];
                                          'MAN':
                                            PackageTrackingNo := CKElement[3];
                                          'N1':
                                            BEGIN
                                              IF CKElement[2] = 'ST' THEN BEGIN
                                                STOn := TRUE;
                                                EVALUATE(SalesHeader."Ship-to Name",CKElement[3]);
                                              END ELSE
                                                STOn := FALSE;
                                              IF NOT STOn AND (CKElement[2] = 'BT') THEN BEGIN
                                                IF STRLEN(CKElement[5]) < 5 THEN
                                                  CKElement[5] := COPYSTR('00000', 1, 5 - STRLEN(CKElement[5])) + CKElement[5];
                                                EVALUATE(CustNo,CKElement[5]);

                                                SalesHeader.INIT;
                                                SalesHeader.SetHideValidationDialog(TRUE);
                                                SalesHeader."Document Type" := SalesHeader."Document Type"::Order;
                                                SalesHeader."No." := '';
                                                SalesHeader.INSERT(TRUE);
                                                SalesHeader."Warehouse Release No." := FORMAT(ReleaseNo);
                                                IF Cust.GET(CustNo) THEN
                                                  SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Sell-to Customer No.",CustNo)
                                                ELSE
                                                  SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Sell-to Customer No.",'00000');
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 5 Code",'E');
                                                SalesHeader."Document Date" := BatchDate;
                                                SalesHeader."Order Date" := OrderDate;
                                                // <TPZHOTFIX>
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Location Code",LocationCode);
                                                // </TPZHOTFIX>
                                                SalesHeader."External Document No." := ExternalDocumentNo;
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shipment Date",ShipmentDate);

                                                IF LocSASMpng.GET(LocationCode,ShippingAgentAndService) THEN BEGIN
                                                  SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shipping Agent Code",LocSASMpng."Shipping Agent Code");
                                                  SalesHeader.VALIDATE("E-Ship Agent Service",LocSASMpng."E-Ship Agent Service");
                                                END ELSE
                                                  IF STRPOS(ShippingAgentAndService,'UPS') <> 0 THEN
                                                    SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shipping Agent Code",'UPS');
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Package Tracking No.",PackageTrackingNo);
                                                SalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                              END;
                                            END;
                                          'N3':
                                            IF STOn THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesHeader."Ship-to Address" := CKElement[2];
                                              SalesHeader."Ship-to Address 2" := CKElement[3];
                                              SalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                            END;
                                          'N4':
                                            IF STOn THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesHeader."Ship-to City" := CKElement[2];
                                              SalesHeader."Ship-to County" := CKElement[3];
                                              SalesHeader."Ship-to Post Code" := CKElement[4];
                                              SalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                            END;
                                          'PO1':
                                            BEGIN
                                              SalesLine2.RESET;
                                              SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                                              SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
                                              IF SalesLine2.FINDLAST THEN
                                                LineNo := SalesLine2."Line No." + 10000
                                              ELSE
                                                LineNo := 10000;

                                              SalesLine.INIT;
                                              SalesLine."Document Type" := SalesHeader."Document Type";
                                              SalesLine."Document No." := SalesHeader."No.";
                                              SalesLine."Line No." := LineNo;
                                              SalesLine.INSERT(TRUE);
                                              SalesLine."Sell-to Customer No." := SalesHeader."Sell-to Customer No.";
                                              SalesLine.Type := SalesLine.Type::Item;

                                              EVALUATE(ItemNo,CKElement[8]);
                                              IF Item.GET(ItemNo) THEN
                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE("No.",ItemNo);
                                              //<TPZ2558>
                                              IF Item."Shortcut Dimension 5 Code" = 'P' THEN BEGIN
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 5 Code",'P');
                                                SalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                              END;
                                            //</TPZ2558>
                                              //<TPZ1312>
                                              //EVALUATE(ExternalDocumentLineNo,CKElement[2]);
                                              ExternalDocumentLineNo := CKElement[2];
                                              //</TPZ1312>

                                              SalesLine."External Document Line No." := ExternalDocumentLineNo;

                                              EVALUATE(UnitOfMeasure,CKElement[4]);

                                              EVALUATE(QuantityOrdered,CKElement[3]);

                                              EVALUATE(UnitPrice,CKElement[5]);
                                              UnitPrice := ROUND(UnitPrice / 10000,0.0001);

                                              IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item) AND
                                                 (SalesLine."No." <> '')
                                              THEN BEGIN
                                                IF UnitOfMeasure = 'EA' THEN
                                                  SalesLine.VALIDATE("Unit of Measure Code",'PCS');

                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE(Quantity,QuantityOrdered);

                                                IF SalesLine."Unit Price" <> 0 THEN
                                                  Multiplier := UnitPrice / SalesLine."Unit Price"
                                                ELSE
                                                  Multiplier := 1;

                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE("Actual Unit Price",UnitPrice);
                                                //<TPZ1125>
                                                //SalesLine."Unit Price Color":=SalesLine.SetStyle;
                                                 SalesLine."Unit Price Color":= Table37EventSubscribers.Tb37_SetStyle(SalesLine); //TPZ2829 Event Conversion
                                                //</TPZ1125>
                                              END;

                                              SalesLine.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                            END;
                                          'PID':
                                            BEGIN
                                              EVALUATE(Description,COPYSTR(CKElement[6],1,MAXSTRLEN(Description)));
                                              SalesLine.Description := Description;
                                            END;
                                          'IT3':
                                            BEGIN
                                              EVALUATE(QuantityShipped,CKElement[2]);
                                              IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item) AND
                                                 (SalesLine."No." <> '')
                                              THEN BEGIN
                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE("Qty. to Ship",QuantityShipped);
                                                SalesLine.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                              END;

                                              WhseReleaseLine.INIT;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Location Code" := SalesHeader."Location Code";
                                              WhseReleaseLine."File Name" := xFile.Name;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Batch Date" := BatchDate;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Batch Time" := BatchTime;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Release No." := ReleaseNo;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Customer No." := CustNo;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Order Date" := OrderDate;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."External Document No." := ExternalDocumentNo;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Shipping Agent and Service" := ShippingAgentAndService;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Shipping Payment Type" := ShippingPaymentType;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Package Tracking No." := PackageTrackingNo;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Backorder No." := BackorderNo;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Shipment Date" := ShipmentDate;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Freight Charge Amt." := FreightChargeAmt;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Name" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Name";
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Address" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Address";
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Address 2" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Address 2";
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to City" := SalesHeader."Ship-to City";
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to County" := SalesHeader."Ship-to County";
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Post Code" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Post Code";
                                              WhseReleaseLine."External Document Line No." := ExternalDocumentLineNo;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Item No." := ItemNo;
                                              WhseReleaseLine.Description := Description;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."UOM Code" := UnitOfMeasure;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Ordered" := QuantityOrdered;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Shipped" := QuantityShipped;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Backordered" := QuantityBackordered;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Whse. Backordered" := QuantityWhseBackordered;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Unit Price" := UnitPrice;
                                              WhseReleaseLine."Mfr. Rep. Code" := SalesHeader."Mfr. Rep. Code";

                                              IF WhseReleaseLine.INSERT THEN
                                                WhseReleaseLine.MODIFY;
                                            END;
                                          'CTT':
                                            BEGIN
                                              IF FreightChargeAmt <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                                SalesSetup.GET;
                                                SalesSetup.TESTFIELD(SalesSetup."Freight G/L Acc. No.");

                                                SalesLine2.RESET;
                                                SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                                                SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
                                                IF SalesLine2.FINDLAST THEN
                                                  LineNo := SalesLine2."Line No." + 10000
                                                ELSE
                                                  LineNo := 10000;

                                                SalesLine.INIT;
                                                SalesLine."Document Type" := SalesHeader."Document Type";
                                                SalesLine."Document No." := SalesHeader."No.";
                                                SalesLine."Line No." := LineNo;
                                                SalesLine.INSERT(TRUE);
                                                SalesLine."Sell-to Customer No." := SalesHeader."Sell-to Customer No.";
                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE(Type,SalesLine.Type::"G/L Account");
                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE("No.", SalesSetup."Freight G/L Acc. No.");
                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE(Quantity,1);
                                                SalesLine.VALIDATE("Unit Price",FreightChargeAmt);
                                                SalesLine.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                              END;
                                              COMMIT;
                                            END;
                                        END;

                                        l := 1;
                                        CLEAR(CKElement[l]);
                                      END ELSE
                                        IF (Char = 10) OR (Char = 13) THEN BEGIN
                                          l := 1;
                                          i := 0;
                                          k := 0;
                                        END ELSE BEGIN
                                          k := k + 1;
                                          CodeString[k] := Char;
                                        END;
                                  UNTIL j = 1;
                                  CommonInpFile.CLOSE;

                                  FILE.COPY(xFile.Path + xFile.Name,xFile.Path + 'Archive\' + xFile.Name);
                                  ERASE(xFile.Path + xFile.Name);
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1000000001;1;Column;xFileName          ;
               SourceExpr=xFile.Name }

    { 1000000002;1;Column;BatchDate          ;

    { 1000000049;1;Column;LocationCode       ;
               SourceExpr=LocationCode }

               DataItemTable=Table50043;

    PROCEDURE ClearTailSpace@1000000003(String@1000000000 : Text[80]) TextString : Text[80];
    VAR
      Xtmp@1000000002 : Text[80];
      i@1000000001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      i := STRLEN(String);
      Xtmp := '';
      TextString := '';
      REPEAT
        Xtmp := COPYSTR(String,i,1);
        IF Xtmp = ' ' THEN
          i := i - 1;
      UNTIL (Xtmp <> ' ') OR (i=0);
      IF i = 0 THEN
        TextString := ''
      ELSE
        TextString := COPYSTR(String,1,i);
    END;

    PROCEDURE Trim@1000000000(String@1000000000 : Text[250]) : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELCHR(String,'<>',' '));
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
